{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-sonnet-4-6","id":"msg_01D39i97kAwaF1xSTwejfvQQ","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_015QubtAtukF2NxBAmvMwiTr","name":"Write","input":{"path":"/workspace/docs/gdscript_vm_reference.md","content":"# GDScript VM Bytecode Instruction Set Reference\n\n> **Source files:**\n> - `modules/gdscript/gdscript_function.h` — opcode enum, address encoding, `GDScriptFunction` structure\n> - `modules/gdscript/gdscript_vm.cpp` — interpreter dispatch loop and per-opcode semantics\n> - `modules/gdscript/gdscript_compiler.cpp` — bytecode generation (AST → opcodes)\n\n---\n\n## 1. VM Architecture\n\nThe GDScript virtual machine is **register-based with a flat Variant array** (commonly called \"the stack\" in the source, but individual operands are addressed by index rather than pushed/popped).\n\nKey characteristics:\n\n| Property | Value |\n|---|---|\n| Architecture | Register / flat-array (not a push-pop stack) |\n| Value type | `Variant` (tagged union covering all GDScript types) |\n| Word size | `int` (32-bit opcode words) |\n| Instruction pointer | Integer index `ip` into `_code_ptr[]` |\n| Max call depth | 2 048 frames (enforced per-thread) |\n| Dispatch | Computed-goto table on GCC; `switch` on MSVC |\n\n### Runtime Layout\n\nAt function entry the VM allocates a single contiguous block via `alloca()`:\n\n```\n[0 .. _stack_size-1]          Variant[_stack_size]   (working registers)\n[sizeof(Variant)*_stack_size] Variant*[_instruction_args_size]  (per-instruction argument pointer array)\n```\n\nThe first three stack slots are **fixed** (see §3 below); user registers begin at slot 3.\n\n---\n\n## 2. Address Encoding\n\nEvery operand in the bytecode stream is encoded as a single `int` word with the following bit layout:\n\n```\n  bits 31..24  bits 23..0\n ┌────────────┬────────────────────────────┐\n │ addr_type  │      addr_index (24 bits)  │\n └────────────┴────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\nConstants from `GDScriptFunction::Address` (`gdscript_function.h:373`):\n\n| Constant | Value | Meaning |\n|---|---|---|\n| `ADDR_BITS` | 24 | Index occupies the low 24 bits |\n| `ADDR_MASK` | `(1<<24)-1` | Mask for the index |\n| `ADDR_TYPE_MASK` | `~ADDR_MASK` | Mask for the type tag |\n| `ADDR_TYPE_STACK` | 0 | Operand lives in the stack/register array |\n| `ADDR_TYPE_CONSTANT` | 1 | Operand is a compile-time constant (`_constants_ptr[]`) |\n| `ADDR_TYPE_MEMBER` | 2 | Operand is an instance member (`p_instance->members[]`) |\n| `ADDR_TYPE_MAX` | 3 | Sentinel |\n\nAt runtime the macro `GET_VARIANT_PTR(name, offset)` decodes `_code_ptr[ip + 1 + offset]` into a `Variant*` by indexing the appropriate array.\n\n### Fixed Stack Addresses\n\n```\nADDR_STACK_SELF  = 0   → stack[0] = p_instance->owner (Object*)\nADDR_STACK_CLASS = 1   → stack[1] = script (GDScript*)\nADDR_STACK_NIL   = 2   → stack[2] = Variant() (null sentinel)\n```\n\nUser locals and temporaries start at stack index 3.\n\n---\n\n## 3. Variant Type System\n\nAll values are `Variant` instances. The `Variant::Type` enum (from `core/variant/variant.h`) includes:\n\n| Type ID | Name |\n|---|---|\n| 0 | `NIL` |\n| 1 | `BOOL` |\n| 2 | `INT` |\n| 3 | `FLOAT` |\n| 4 | `STRING` |\n| 5 | `VECTOR2` |\n| 6 | `VECTOR2I` |\n| 7 | `RECT2` |\n| 8 | `RECT2I` |\n| 9 | `VECTOR3` |\n| 10 | `VECTOR3I` |\n| 11 | `TRANSFORM2D` |\n| 12 | `VECTOR4` |\n| 13 | `VECTOR4I` |\n| 14 | `PLANE` |\n| 15 | `QUATERNION` |\n| 16 | `AABB` |\n| 17 | `BASIS` |\n| 18 | `TRANSFORM3D` |\n| 19 | `PROJECTION` |\n| 20 | `COLOR` |\n| 21 | `STRING_NAME` |\n| 22 | `NODE_PATH` |\n| 23 | `RID` |\n| 24 | `OBJECT` |\n| 25 | `CALLABLE` |\n| 26 | `SIGNAL` |\n| 27 | `DICTIONARY` |\n| 28 | `ARRAY` |\n| 29–38 | Packed arrays (`PACKED_BYTE_ARRAY` … `PACKED_VECTOR4_ARRAY`) |\n\nType-checking is performed by `GDScriptDataType::is_type()` (`gdscript_function.h:67`). The type descriptor's `kind` field distinguishes `BUILTIN`, `NATIVE`, `SCRIPT`, and `GDSCRIPT`.\n\n---\n\n## 4. Complete Opcode Table\n\nOpcodes are defined as `GDScriptFunction::Opcode` (`gdscript_function.h:218`). Below each opcode shows:\n- **Operand words** after the opcode word (encoded addresses use `GET_VARIANT_PTR`; plain integers are raw `int` values in `_code_ptr[]`)\n- **Semantics** derived from the dispatch loop in `gdscript_vm.cpp`\n\n### 4.1 Arithmetic / Bitwise / Comparison Operators\n\n| Opcode | Extra words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_OPERATOR` | `a_addr, b_addr, dst_addr, op, sig_cache, ret_type_cache, func_ptr…` | `*dst = *a OP *b`. The `op` field is `Variant::Operator`. On first execution records the validated function pointer inline (\"inline caching\"). Falls back to `Variant::evaluate()` on type mismatch. |\n| `OPCODE_OPERATOR_VALIDATED` | `a_addr, b_addr, dst_addr, func_idx` | Pre-validated fast path. Calls `_operator_funcs_ptr[func_idx](a, b, dst)`. |\n\nThe `op` word for `OPCODE_OPERATOR` maps to `Variant::Operator` values: `OP_ADD`, `OP_SUBTRACT`, `OP_MULTIPLY`, `OP_DIVIDE`, `OP_MODULE`, `OP_EQUAL`, `OP_NOT_EQUAL`, `OP_LESS`, `OP_LESS_EQUAL`, `OP_GREATER`, `OP_GREATER_EQUAL`, `OP_AND`, `OP_OR`, `OP_NOT`, `OP_IN`, `OP_SHIFT_LEFT`, `OP_SHIFT_RIGHT`, `OP_BIT_AND`, `OP_BIT_OR`, `OP_BIT_XOR`, `OP_BIT_NEGATE`.\n\n### 4.2 Type Tests\n\n| Opcode | Extra words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_TYPE_TEST_BUILTIN` | `dst_addr, value_addr, builtin_type` | `*dst = (value->get_type() == builtin_type)` |\n| `OPCODE_TYPE_TEST_ARRAY` | `dst_addr, value_addr, script_type_addr, builtin_type, native_type_idx` | Tests typed-array element type. |\n| `OPCODE_TYPE_TEST_NATIVE` | `dst_addr, value_addr, native_type_idx` | `*dst = ClassDB::is_parent_class(obj->class_name, native_type)` |\n| `OPCODE_TYPE_TEST_SCRIPT` | `dst_addr, value_addr, type_addr` | Walks the script inheritance chain. |\n\nThese implement GDScript's `is` operator.\n\n### 4.3 Key/Index/Named Access\n\n| Opcode | Extra words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_GET_KEYED` | `src_addr, index_addr, dst_addr` | `*dst = src->get(*index)` — dynamic/slow path. |\n| `OPCODE_GET_KEYED_VALIDATED` | `src_addr, key_addr, dst_addr, getter_idx` | `_keyed_getters_ptr[getter_idx](src, key, dst, &valid)` |\n| `OPCODE_GET_INDEXED_VALIDATED` | `src_addr, index_addr, dst_addr, getter_idx` | Integer-indexed fast path. |\n| `OPCODE_SET_KEYED` | `dst_addr, index_addr, value_addr` | `dst->set(*index, *value)` |\n| `OPCODE_SET_KEYED_VALIDATED` | `dst_addr, index_addr, value_addr, setter_idx` | |\n| `OPCODE_SET_INDEXED_VALIDATED` | `dst_addr, index_addr, value_addr, setter_idx` | Integer-indexed. |\n| `OPCODE_GET_NAMED` | `src_addr, dst_addr, name_idx` | `*dst = src->get_named(_global_names_ptr[name_idx])` |\n| `OPCODE_GET_NAMED_VALIDATED` | `src_addr, dst_addr, getter_idx` | `_getters_ptr[getter_idx](src, dst)` |\n| `OPCODE_SET_NAMED` | `dst_addr, value_addr, name_idx` | `dst->set_named(_global_names_ptr[name_idx], *value)` |\n| `OPCODE_SET_NAMED_VALIDATED` | `dst_addr, value_addr, setter_idx` | `_setters_ptr[setter_idx](dst, value)` |\n\n`_global_names_ptr[]` is a compile-time `StringName[]` table embedded in the function object.\n\n### 4.4 Member / Static Variable Access\n\n| Opcode | Extra words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_GET_MEMBER` | `dst_addr, name_idx` | `ClassDB::get_property(p_instance->owner, name, *dst)` — native property getter. |\n| `OPCODE_SET_MEMBER` | `src_addr, name_idx` | `ClassDB::set_property(p_instance->owner, name, *src)` |\n| `OPCODE_GET_STATIC_VARIABLE` | `target_addr, class_addr, var_idx` | `*target = gdscript->static_variables[var_idx]` |\n| `OPCODE_SET_STATIC_VARIABLE` | `value_addr, class_addr, var_idx` | `gdscript->static_variables[var_idx] = *value` |\n\nInstance member variables (GDScript-level fields) are accessed via `ADDR_TYPE_MEMBER` addressing directly; `GET_MEMBER`/`SET_MEMBER` are for **native (C++) properties** defined on the base class.\n\n### 4.5 Assignment\n\n| Opcode | Extra words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN` | `dst_addr, src_addr` | `*dst = *src` |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_NULL` | `dst_addr` | `*dst = Variant()` |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_TRUE` | `dst_addr` | `*dst = true` |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_FALSE` | `dst_addr` | `*dst = false` |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_TYPED_BUILTIN` | `dst_addr, src_addr, type` | Type-checked copy; constructs via `Variant::construct()` if types differ. |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_TYPED_ARRAY` | `dst_addr, src_addr, script_type_addr, builtin_type, native_type_idx` | Verifies typed-array element type before copying. |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_TYPED_NATIVE` | `dst_addr, src_addr, native_class_addr` | Verifies object is an instance of the native class. |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_TYPED_SCRIPT` | `dst_addr, src_addr, script_addr` | Walks GDScript inheritance chain to verify compatibility. |\n\n### 4.6 Type Casts\n\n| Opcode | Extra words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_CAST_TO_BUILTIN` | `src_addr, dst_addr, type` | `Variant::construct(type, *dst, &src, 1, err)` |\n| `OPCODE_CAST_TO_NATIVE` | `src_addr, dst_addr, native_class_addr` | Sets `*dst = null` if object doesn't inherit the target class; otherwise copies. |\n| `OPCODE_CAST_TO_SCRIPT` | `src_addr, dst_addr, script_addr` | Same semantics, for GDScript types. |\n\n### 4.7 Construction\n\n| Opcode | Extra words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT` | `[arg_addrs…], argc, type` | `Variant::construct(type, *dst, argptrs, argc, err)` |\n| `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_VALIDATED` | `[arg_addrs…], argc, ctor_idx` | `_constructors_ptr[ctor_idx](dst, argptrs)` |\n| `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_ARRAY` | `[elem_addrs…], argc` | Builds an untyped `Array` from `argc` elements. |\n| `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_TYPED_ARRAY` | `[elem_addrs…], argc, script_type_addr, builtin_type, native_type_idx` | Builds a typed `Array`. |\n| `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_DICTIONARY` | `[k0_addr, v0_addr, …], argc` | Builds a `Dictionary`; operands alternate key/value pairs; `argc` is the number of key-value pairs. |\n\nFor variable-argument instructions the VM first calls `LOAD_INSTRUCTION_ARGS`, which reads `_code_ptr[ip+1]` as the argument count and populates `instruction_args[]` before advancing `ip`.\n\n### 4.8 Function Calls\n\nAll call instructions use the `LOAD_INSTRUCTION_ARGS` / `GET_INSTRUCTION_ARG` protocol. Arguments are stored in `instruction_args[0..argc-1]`, the **base object** (receiver) at `instruction_args[argc]`, and the return slot (when present) at `instruction_args[argc+1]`.\n\n| Opcode | Extra words (after arg block) | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_CALL` | `argc, name_idx` | `base->callp(name, argptrs, argc, ret, err)` — no return captured. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_RETURN` | `argc, name_idx` | Same but captures return value into `instruction_args[argc+1]`. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_ASYNC` | `argc, name_idx` | Like `CALL_RETURN` but suppresses the \"async without await\" error. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_UTILITY` | `argc, name_idx` | `Variant::call_utility_function(name, dst, argptrs, argc, err)` — global utility (e.g. `print`, `len`). |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_UTILITY_VALIDATED` | `argc, utility_idx` | `_utilities_ptr[utility_idx](dst, argptrs, argc)` |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_GDSCRIPT_UTILITY` | `argc, gds_util_idx` | GDScript-specific utilities via `_gds_utilities_ptr[]`. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_BUILTIN_TYPE_VALIDATED` | `argc, method_idx` | `_builtin_methods_ptr[method_idx](base, argptrs, argc, ret)` — method on a Variant builtin type. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_SELF_BASE` | `argc, name_idx` | Walks `_script->base` chain to call parent-class method. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_METHOD_BIND` | `argc, method_idx` | `_methods_ptr[method_idx]->call(base_obj, argptrs, argc, err)` — no return. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_METHOD_BIND_RET` | `argc, method_idx` | Same, captures return. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_METHOD_BIND_VALIDATED_RETURN` | `argc, method_idx` | `method->validated_call(base_obj, argptrs, ret)` — bypasses CallError struct. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_METHOD_BIND_VALIDATED_NO_RETURN` | `argc, method_idx` | Same without return. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_BUILTIN_STATIC` | `builtin_type, name_idx, argc` | `Variant::call_static(builtin_type, name, argptrs, argc, ret, err)` |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_NATIVE_STATIC` | `method_idx, argc` | `_methods_ptr[method_idx]->call(nullptr, argptrs, argc, err)` |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_NATIVE_STATIC_VALIDATED_RETURN` | `argc, method_idx` | `method->validated_call(nullptr, argptrs, ret)` |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_NATIVE_STATIC_VALIDATED_NO_RETURN` | `argc, method_idx` | Same, discards return. |\n\n**Validated vs. unvalidated calls:** When the compiler can prove argument types match exactly (via `_can_use_validate_call()`), it emits a `*_VALIDATED_*` opcode that bypasses `Callable::CallError` checking for better performance.\n\n### 4.9 Async / Coroutine\n\n| Opcode | Extra words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_AWAIT` | `signal_or_state_addr` | Suspends execution. If operand is a `Signal` or `GDScriptFunctionState`, connects a one-shot callback and returns a `GDScriptFunctionState` from the outer `call()`. If operand is an immediate value, falls through by skipping `OPCODE_AWAIT_RESUME`. |\n| `OPCODE_AWAIT_RESUME` | `result_addr` | Written immediately after `OPCODE_AWAIT` in the stream. On resume, copies `p_state->result` into `*result`. |\n\n### 4.10 Lambda Creation\n\n| Opcode | Extra words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_CREATE_LAMBDA` | `[capture_addrs…], captures_count, lambda_idx` | Creates a `GDScriptLambdaCallable` that closes over `captures_count` values. Result is a `Callable`. |\n| `OPCODE_CREATE_SELF_LAMBDA` | `[capture_addrs…], captures_count, lambda_idx` | Same but binds `self` (for non-static lambdas). Creates `GDScriptLambdaSelfCallable`. |\n\n### 4.11 Control Flow\n\n| Opcode | Extra words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_JUMP` | `target` | `ip = target` (absolute code offset). |\n| `OPCODE_JUMP_IF` | `test_addr, target` | `if (test->booleanize()) ip = target` |\n| `OPCODE_JUMP_IF_NOT` | `test_addr, target` | `if (!test->booleanize()) ip = target` |\n| `OPCODE_JUMP_TO_DEF_ARGUMENT` | _(none)_ | `ip = _default_arg_ptr[defarg]` — jumps to the initializer for the next missing default argument. |\n| `OPCODE_JUMP_IF_SHARED` | `val_addr, target` | `if (val->is_shared()) ip = target` — used to implement copy-on-write semantics before mutation. |\n\n### 4.12 Return\n\n| Opcode | Extra words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_RETURN` | `value_addr` | `retvalue = *r; OPCODE_BREAK` — exits the dispatch loop. |\n| `OPCODE_RETURN_TYPED_BUILTIN` | `value_addr, type` | Returns after type-checking / coercing to built-in type. |\n| `OPCODE_RETURN_TYPED_ARRAY` | `value_addr, script_type_addr, builtin_type, native_type_idx` | Validates typed array before returning. |\n| `OPCODE_RETURN_TYPED_NATIVE` | `value_addr, native_class_addr` | Validates Object subclass. |\n| `OPCODE_RETURN_TYPED_SCRIPT` | `value_addr, script_addr` | Validates GDScript subtype. |\n\n### 4.13 Iteration (`for` Loops)\n\nThe `for x in collection` construct compiles to an `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_*` followed by a loop that calls `OPCODE_ITERATE_*`. The `_BEGIN_` variant initialises the iterator state; the non-`_BEGIN_` variant advances and writes the next value or jumps to the exit.\n\nBoth instruction families share the format:\n\n```\nOPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_<TYPE>   counter_addr, container_addr, value_addr, exit_offset\nOPCODE_ITERATE_<TYPE>         counter_addr, container_addr, value_addr, exit_offset\n```\n\n| Type suffix | Container type |\n|---|---|\n| _(none)_ | Generic `Variant` (slow, dynamic dispatch) |\n| `_INT` | `int` range |\n| `_FLOAT` | `float` range |\n| `_VECTOR2` | `Vector2` |\n| `_VECTOR2I` | `Vector2i` |\n| `_VECTOR3` | `Vector3` |\n| `_VECTOR3I` | `Vector3i` |\n| `_STRING` | `String` (character iteration) |\n| `_DICTIONARY` | `Dictionary` (key iteration) |\n| `_ARRAY` | `Array` |\n| `_PACKED_BYTE_ARRAY` | `PackedByteArray` |\n| `_PACKED_INT32_ARRAY` | `PackedInt32Array` |\n| `_PACKED_INT64_ARRAY` | `PackedInt64Array` |\n| `_PACKED_FLOAT32_ARRAY` | `PackedFloat32Array` |\n| `_PACKED_FLOAT64_ARRAY` | `PackedFloat64Array` |\n| `_PACKED_STRING_ARRAY` | `PackedStringArray` |\n| `_PACKED_VECTOR2_ARRAY` | `PackedVector2Array` |\n| `_PACKED_VECTOR3_ARRAY` | `PackedVector3Array` |\n| `_PACKED_COLOR_ARRAY` | `PackedColorArray` |\n| `_PACKED_VECTOR4_ARRAY` | `PackedVector4Array` |\n| `_OBJECT` | Objects implementing `_iter_init` / `_iter_next` / `_iter_get` |\n\nWhen the iterator is exhausted the VM jumps to `ip + exit_offset` (loop exit).\n\n### 4.14 Global / Named Global Storage\n\n| Opcode | Extra words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_STORE_GLOBAL` | `dst_addr, global_idx` | Copies a value from the global constant table (by integer index) into `*dst`. |\n| `OPCODE_STORE_NAMED_GLOBAL` | `dst_addr, name_idx` | Looks up a global by `StringName` in `GDScriptLanguage::get_singleton()->get_global_map()`. |\n\n### 4.15 Type Adjustment\n\n`OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_<TYPE>` opcodes re-initialise a stack slot in-place to ensure it holds the correct concrete C++ type inside the `Variant` wrapper. This is needed when a temporary slot is reused across different typed contexts.\n\nOne opcode exists for every `Variant::Type` value. Format:\n\n```\nOPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_<TYPE>   target_addr\n```\n\nSemantics: `VariantInternal::initialize(target, Variant::TYPE_<TYPE>)` — resets the variant's internal storage without changing its address.\n\n### 4.16 Debug / Metadata\n\n| Opcode | Extra words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_ASSERT` | `value_addr, message_addr` | Evaluates condition; on failure prints message and breaks. Compiled away in release builds. |\n| `OPCODE_BREAKPOINT` | _(none)_ | Triggers the debugger breakpoint handler. |\n| `OPCODE_LINE` | `line_number` | Records the current source line for error messages and the debugger. No runtime effect otherwise. |\n| `OPCODE_END` | _(none)_ | Implicit end of function body; control should never reach this in correct code. |\n\n---\n\n## 5. Function Call Convention\n\n### 5.1 Calling a GDScript Function\n\nEntry point: `GDScriptFunction::call()` (`gdscript_vm.cpp:448`).\n\n```\nVariant call(GDScriptInstance *p_instance,\n             const Variant    **p_args,\n             int                p_argcount,\n             Callable::CallError &r_err,\n             CallState          *p_state = nullptr);\n```\n\n**Frame setup:**\n\n1. `alloca_size = sizeof(Variant*) * 3 + sizeof(Variant*) * _instruction_args_size + sizeof(Variant) * _stack_size`\n2. Arguments `p_args[0..p_argcount-1]` are placement-new'd into `stack[3..3+p_argcount-1]` with optional type coercion.\n3. Remaining slots `stack[p_argcount+3.._stack_size-1]` are zero-initialised.\n4. `stack[0]` = `p_instance->owner` (self), `stack[1]` = `script`, `stack[2]` = `Variant()` (nil).\n5. Temporaries listed in `temporary_slots` are initialised via `type_init_function_table[type](&stack[slot])`.\n\n**Default arguments:**\n\nIf `p_argcount < _argument_count`, `defarg = _argument_count - p_argcount`. The VM enters the function at the normal start but encounters `OPCODE_JUMP_TO_DEF_ARGUMENT` which re-directs `ip` to `_default_arg_ptr[defarg]` to initialise the missing argument, then falls through to normal code.\n\n**Return:**\n\n`OPCODE_RETURN` (and the typed variants) set `retvalue` then break out of the dispatch loop. The return value is the function's stack-local `Variant retvalue`.\n\n**Maximum recursion:** Each frame increments a thread-local `call_depth`. If it exceeds `MAX_CALL_DEPTH` (2 048), the call returns a default-constructed value and sets `r_err`.\n\n### 5.2 Calling a Native Method (MethodBind)\n\n- **`OPCODE_CALL_METHOD_BIND_RET`** — `method->call(base_obj, argptrs, argc, err)` via `Callable::CallError`.\n- **`OPCODE_CALL_METHOD_BIND_VALIDATED_RETURN`** — `method->validated_call(base_obj, argptrs, ret)` (no error struct, faster).\n\nThe compiler chooses the validated form when it can prove all argument types match the method's signature exactly (`_can_use_validate_call()`, `gdscript_compiler.cpp:234`).\n\n### 5.3 Argument Passing for Variable-Argument Instructions\n\nInstructions that accept a variable number of operands (calls, constructs, etc.) use a two-level scheme:\n\n1. **Load phase** (`LOAD_INSTRUCTION_ARGS`): reads `_code_ptr[ip+1]` as the count, then calls `GET_VARIANT_PTR` for each argument to populate `instruction_args[]` with `Variant*` pointers.\n2. **Access phase** (`GET_INSTRUCTION_ARG(v, idx)`): `Variant *v = instruction_args[idx]`.\n\nAfter loading, `ip` is incremented by `instr_arg_count` so subsequent `_code_ptr[ip + N]` words refer to the fixed (non-address) parameters (argc, method index, etc.).\n\n---\n\n## 6. Local Variable and Member Variable Access\n\n### 6.1 Local Variables and Parameters\n\nBoth function parameters and local variables reside in the same flat stack array, starting at index 3 (after the three fixed slots). Parameters are placed at `stack[3], stack[4], …` and locals occupy higher indices as determined by the compiler's `CodeGen` allocation.\n\nThe compiler tracks these in `codegen.parameters` and `codegen.locals` (`gdscript_compiler.cpp:70`). When referenced in an expression, they are returned as `Address(ADDR_TYPE_STACK, idx)`.\n\n### 6.2 Instance Member Variables\n\nGDScript instance member variables are stored in `GDScriptInstance::members[]` (a `Vector<Variant>`). They are accessed via the `ADDR_TYPE_MEMBER` address type:\n\n```\naddress = member_index | (ADDR_TYPE_MEMBER << ADDR_BITS)\n```\n\nAt runtime, `variant_addresses[ADDR_TYPE_MEMBER] = p_instance->members.ptrw()`.\n\n### 6.3 Native (C++) Properties\n\nNative properties (registered with `ClassDB`) are accessed via `OPCODE_GET_MEMBER` / `OPCODE_SET_MEMBER`, which delegate to `ClassDB::get_property()` / `ClassDB::set_property()`.\n\nWhen a GDScript member has a custom getter/setter function, the compiler emits `OPCODE_CALL_SELF_BASE` (or `write_call_self`) to call the accessor rather than accessing the backing slot directly (`gdscript_compiler.cpp:303`).\n\n### 6.4 Static Variables\n\nGDScript static variables live in `GDScript::static_variables[]`. They are accessed via `OPCODE_GET_STATIC_VARIABLE` / `OPCODE_SET_STATIC_VARIABLE`, which locate the owning `GDScript` object from `stack[ADDR_STACK_CLASS]` and index into its `static_variables` array.\n\n### 6.5 Constants\n\nCompile-time constants (literals, folded expressions) are stored in `GDScriptFunction::constants[]` and referenced via `ADDR_TYPE_CONSTANT` addresses. They are immutable during execution.\n\n---\n\n## 7. Dispatch Loop Implementation\n\nOn GCC/Clang, the VM uses a **computed-goto dispatch table** (`OPCODES_TABLE` macro, `gdscript_vm.cpp:214`):\n\n```c\nstatic const void *switch_table_ops[] = { &&OPCODE_OPERATOR, &&OPCODE_OPERATOR_VALIDATED, … };\n// At each opcode end:\ngoto *switch_table_ops[_code_ptr[ip]];\n```\n\nOn MSVC (and as fallback), a `switch` statement is used instead. Both paths are abstracted by the `OPCODE`, `OPCODE_SWITCH`, `DISPATCH_OPCODE`, and related macros.\n\nThe outer loop guard is:\n- **Debug builds:** `while (ip < _code_size)` — bounds-checked.\n- **Release builds:** `while (true)` — no check; relies on `OPCODE_RETURN`/`OPCODE_END` to exit.\n\n---\n\n## 8. Coroutine / Await Suspension State\n\nWhen `OPCODE_AWAIT` suspends a function, the entire execution state is captured into a heap-allocated `GDScriptFunctionState` (`gdscript_function.h:558`):\n\n```cpp\nstruct CallState {\n    GDScript         *script;\n    GDScriptInstance *instance;\n    Vector<uint8_t>   stack;   // serialised Variant array\n    int               stack_size, ip, line, defarg;\n    Variant           result;  // value injected on resume\n};\n```\n\nStack slots 3 through `_stack_size-1` are placement-new'd into `gdfs->state.stack`. On `resume()`, the state is passed back as `p_state` and the VM restores the previous frame, continuing at `ip` pointing to `OPCODE_AWAIT_RESUME`.\n\n---\n\n## 9. Summary: Opcode Categories\n\n| Category | Opcodes |\n|---|---|\n| Arithmetic/bitwise/comparison | `OPCODE_OPERATOR`, `OPCODE_OPERATOR_VALIDATED` |\n| Type tests (`is`) | `OPCODE_TYPE_TEST_BUILTIN/ARRAY/NATIVE/SCRIPT` |\n| Key/index get | `OPCODE_GET_KEYED`, `OPCODE_GET_KEYED_VALIDATED`, `OPCODE_GET_INDEXED_VALIDATED` |\n| Key/index set | `OPCODE_SET_KEYED`, `OPCODE_SET_KEYED_VALIDATED`, `OPCODE_SET_INDEXED_VALIDATED` |\n| Named property get | `OPCODE_GET_NAMED`, `OPCODE_GET_NAMED_VALIDATED` |\n| Named property set | `OPCODE_SET_NAMED`, `OPCODE_SET_NAMED_VALIDATED` |\n| Member / static variable | `OPCODE_{GET,SET}_MEMBER`, `OPCODE_{GET,SET}_STATIC_VARIABLE` |\n| Assignment | `OPCODE_ASSIGN*` (6 variants) |\n| Type cast | `OPCODE_CAST_TO_BUILTIN/NATIVE/SCRIPT` |\n| Construction | `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT*`, `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_ARRAY*`, `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_DICTIONARY` |\n| Method calls | `OPCODE_CALL*` (15 variants) |\n| Async/coroutine | `OPCODE_AWAIT`, `OPCODE_AWAIT_RESUME` |\n| Lambda creation | `OPCODE_CREATE_LAMBDA`, `OPCODE_CREATE_SELF_LAMBDA` |\n| Control flow | `OPCODE_JUMP*` (5 variants) |\n| Return | `OPCODE_RETURN*` (5 variants) |\n| Iteration | `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_*` / `OPCODE_ITERATE_*` (21 pairs) |\n| Global storage | `OPCODE_STORE_GLOBAL`, `OPCODE_STORE_NAMED_GLOBAL` |\n| Type adjustment | `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_*` (29 variants, one per Variant::Type) |\n| Debug/metadata | `OPCODE_ASSERT`, `OPCODE_BREAKPOINT`, `OPCODE_LINE`, `OPCODE_END` |\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":15211,"cache_read_input_tokens":72691,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":15211,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":9,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"3cf9c07a-6248-4e16-a42f-75e64dcb67f4","uuid":"58eecf64-c792-49e6-99c1-f1a5628a6cc6"}

{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-sonnet-4-6","id":"msg_01VSGmp8E4sJuR7BMMzTE9Bp","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01YaiAmTAfJvrjVxEBKZSyDe","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/docs/gdscript_vm_reference.md","content":"# GDScript VM Bytecode Instruction Set Reference\n\n> **Source files:**\n> - `modules/gdscript/gdscript_function.h` — opcode enum, address encoding, `GDScriptFunction` structure\n> - `modules/gdscript/gdscript_vm.cpp` — interpreter dispatch loop and per-opcode semantics\n> - `modules/gdscript/gdscript_compiler.cpp` — bytecode generation (AST → opcodes)\n\n---\n\n## 1. VM Architecture\n\nThe GDScript virtual machine is **register-based with a flat Variant array** (called \"the stack\" in source, but operands are addressed by index rather than pushed/popped).\n\nKey characteristics:\n\n| Property | Value |\n|---|---|\n| Architecture | Register / flat-array (not a push-pop stack) |\n| Value type | `Variant` (tagged union covering all GDScript types) |\n| Word size | `int` (32-bit opcode words) |\n| Instruction pointer | Integer index `ip` into `_code_ptr[]` |\n| Max call depth | 2 048 frames (enforced per-thread) |\n| Dispatch | Computed-goto table on GCC; `switch` on MSVC |\n\n### Runtime Layout\n\nAt function entry the VM allocates a single contiguous block via `alloca()`:\n\n```\n[0 .. _stack_size-1]                 Variant[_stack_size]              (working registers)\n[sizeof(Variant)*_stack_size ...]    Variant*[_instruction_args_size]  (per-instruction arg pointer array)\n```\n\nThe first three stack slots are **fixed** (see §3); user registers begin at slot 3.\n\n---\n\n## 2. Address Encoding\n\nEvery operand word in the bytecode stream encodes both the storage class and the index:\n\n```\n  bits 31..24      bits 23..0\n ┌────────────┬────────────────────────────┐\n │ addr_type  │      addr_index (24 bits)  │\n └────────────┴────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\nConstants from `GDScriptFunction::Address` (`gdscript_function.h:373`):\n\n| Constant | Value | Meaning |\n|---|---|---|\n| `ADDR_BITS` | 24 | Index occupies the low 24 bits |\n| `ADDR_MASK` | `(1<<24)-1` | Mask for the index |\n| `ADDR_TYPE_MASK` | `~ADDR_MASK` | Mask for the type tag |\n| `ADDR_TYPE_STACK` | 0 | Operand lives in the stack/register array |\n| `ADDR_TYPE_CONSTANT` | 1 | Operand is a compile-time constant (`_constants_ptr[]`) |\n| `ADDR_TYPE_MEMBER` | 2 | Operand is an instance member (`p_instance->members[]`) |\n| `ADDR_TYPE_MAX` | 3 | Sentinel |\n\nAt runtime the macro `GET_VARIANT_PTR(name, offset)` decodes `_code_ptr[ip + 1 + offset]` into a `Variant*` by indexing the appropriate array.\n\n### Fixed Stack Addresses\n\n```\nADDR_STACK_SELF  = 0   →  stack[0] = p_instance->owner  (Object*)\nADDR_STACK_CLASS = 1   →  stack[1] = script              (GDScript*)\nADDR_STACK_NIL   = 2   →  stack[2] = Variant()           (null sentinel)\n```\n\nUser locals and temporaries start at stack index 3.\n\n---\n\n## 3. Variant Type System\n\nAll values are `Variant` instances. The `Variant::Type` enum (from `core/variant/variant.h`) includes:\n\n| Type ID | Name | Notes |\n|---|---|---|\n| 0 | `NIL` | null / unset |\n| 1 | `BOOL` | |\n| 2 | `INT` | `int64_t` |\n| 3 | `FLOAT` | `double` |\n| 4 | `STRING` | |\n| 5–13 | `VECTOR2` … `VECTOR4I` | Math types |\n| 14–19 | `PLANE` … `PROJECTION` | 3-D geometry |\n| 20 | `COLOR` | |\n| 21 | `STRING_NAME` | |\n| 22 | `NODE_PATH` | |\n| 23 | `RID` | |\n| 24 | `OBJECT` | `Object*` (ref-counted or not) |\n| 25 | `CALLABLE` | |\n| 26 | `SIGNAL` | |\n| 27 | `DICTIONARY` | |\n| 28 | `ARRAY` | Optionally typed |\n| 29–38 | `PACKED_*_ARRAY` | Typed contiguous arrays |\n\nType-checking is performed by `GDScriptDataType::is_type()` (`gdscript_function.h:67`). The descriptor's `kind` field distinguishes `BUILTIN`, `NATIVE`, `SCRIPT`, and `GDSCRIPT`.\n\n---\n\n## 4. Complete Opcode Table\n\nOpcodes are defined as `GDScriptFunction::Opcode` (`gdscript_function.h:218`). Each entry shows:\n- **Operand words** after the opcode word (addresses use `GET_VARIANT_PTR`; plain `int` values appear literally in `_code_ptr[]`)\n- **Semantics** derived from the dispatch loop in `gdscript_vm.cpp`\n\n### 4.1 Arithmetic / Bitwise / Comparison Operators\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_OPERATOR` | `a_addr, b_addr, dst_addr, op, sig_cache, ret_type_cache, func_ptr…` | `*dst = *a OP *b`. `op` is `Variant::Operator`. Inline-caches the validated evaluator on first execution; falls back to `Variant::evaluate()` on type mismatch. |\n| `OPCODE_OPERATOR_VALIDATED` | `a_addr, b_addr, dst_addr, func_idx` | Pre-validated fast path: `_operator_funcs_ptr[func_idx](a, b, dst)`. |\n\n`Variant::Operator` values include: `OP_ADD`, `OP_SUBTRACT`, `OP_MULTIPLY`, `OP_DIVIDE`, `OP_MODULE`, `OP_EQUAL`, `OP_NOT_EQUAL`, `OP_LESS`, `OP_LESS_EQUAL`, `OP_GREATER`, `OP_GREATER_EQUAL`, `OP_AND`, `OP_OR`, `OP_NOT`, `OP_IN`, `OP_SHIFT_LEFT`, `OP_SHIFT_RIGHT`, `OP_BIT_AND`, `OP_BIT_OR`, `OP_BIT_XOR`, `OP_BIT_NEGATE`.\n\n### 4.2 Type Tests (`is` operator)\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_TYPE_TEST_BUILTIN` | `dst_addr, value_addr, builtin_type` | `*dst = (value->get_type() == builtin_type)` |\n| `OPCODE_TYPE_TEST_ARRAY` | `dst_addr, value_addr, script_type_addr, builtin_type, native_type_idx` | Tests typed-array element type (builtin type + native class + script). |\n| `OPCODE_TYPE_TEST_NATIVE` | `dst_addr, value_addr, native_type_idx` | `*dst = ClassDB::is_parent_class(obj->class_name, native_type)` |\n| `OPCODE_TYPE_TEST_SCRIPT` | `dst_addr, value_addr, type_addr` | Walks the script inheritance chain. |\n\n### 4.3 Key / Index / Named Access\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_GET_KEYED` | `src_addr, index_addr, dst_addr` | `*dst = src->get(*index)` — dynamic/slow path. |\n| `OPCODE_GET_KEYED_VALIDATED` | `src_addr, key_addr, dst_addr, getter_idx` | `_keyed_getters_ptr[getter_idx](src, key, dst, &valid)` |\n| `OPCODE_GET_INDEXED_VALIDATED` | `src_addr, index_addr, dst_addr, getter_idx` | Integer-indexed fast path. |\n| `OPCODE_SET_KEYED` | `dst_addr, index_addr, value_addr` | `dst->set(*index, *value)` |\n| `OPCODE_SET_KEYED_VALIDATED` | `dst_addr, index_addr, value_addr, setter_idx` | `_keyed_setters_ptr[setter_idx](dst, index, value, &valid)` |\n| `OPCODE_SET_INDEXED_VALIDATED` | `dst_addr, index_addr, value_addr, setter_idx` | Integer-indexed; checks out-of-bounds. |\n| `OPCODE_GET_NAMED` | `src_addr, dst_addr, name_idx` | `*dst = src->get_named(_global_names_ptr[name_idx])` |\n| `OPCODE_GET_NAMED_VALIDATED` | `src_addr, dst_addr, getter_idx` | `_getters_ptr[getter_idx](src, dst)` |\n| `OPCODE_SET_NAMED` | `dst_addr, value_addr, name_idx` | `dst->set_named(_global_names_ptr[name_idx], *value)` |\n| `OPCODE_SET_NAMED_VALIDATED` | `dst_addr, value_addr, setter_idx` | `_setters_ptr[setter_idx](dst, value)` |\n\n`_global_names_ptr[]` is a compile-time `StringName[]` table embedded in the function object.\n\n### 4.4 Member / Static Variable Access\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_GET_MEMBER` | `dst_addr, name_idx` | `ClassDB::get_property(p_instance->owner, name, *dst)` — native C++ property getter. |\n| `OPCODE_SET_MEMBER` | `src_addr, name_idx` | `ClassDB::set_property(p_instance->owner, name, *src)` |\n| `OPCODE_GET_STATIC_VARIABLE` | `target_addr, class_addr, var_idx` | `*target = gdscript->static_variables[var_idx]` |\n| `OPCODE_SET_STATIC_VARIABLE` | `value_addr, class_addr, var_idx` | `gdscript->static_variables[var_idx] = *value` |\n\nGDScript-level instance fields are accessed via `ADDR_TYPE_MEMBER` addressing directly (not through these opcodes). `GET_MEMBER`/`SET_MEMBER` are for **native (C++) properties** registered with `ClassDB`.\n\n### 4.5 Assignment\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN` | `dst_addr, src_addr` | `*dst = *src` |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_NULL` | `dst_addr` | `*dst = Variant()` |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_TRUE` | `dst_addr` | `*dst = true` |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_FALSE` | `dst_addr` | `*dst = false` |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_TYPED_BUILTIN` | `dst_addr, src_addr, type` | Type-checked copy; constructs via `Variant::construct()` if types differ. |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_TYPED_ARRAY` | `dst_addr, src_addr, script_type_addr, builtin_type, native_type_idx` | Verifies typed-array element type before copying. |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_TYPED_NATIVE` | `dst_addr, src_addr, native_class_addr` | Verifies object is an instance of the native class. |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_TYPED_SCRIPT` | `dst_addr, src_addr, script_addr` | Walks GDScript inheritance chain to verify compatibility. |\n\n### 4.6 Type Casts\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_CAST_TO_BUILTIN` | `src_addr, dst_addr, type` | `Variant::construct(type, *dst, &src, 1, err)` |\n| `OPCODE_CAST_TO_NATIVE` | `src_addr, dst_addr, native_class_addr` | Sets `*dst = null` if object doesn't inherit the target class; otherwise copies. |\n| `OPCODE_CAST_TO_SCRIPT` | `src_addr, dst_addr, script_addr` | Same semantics for GDScript types. |\n\n### 4.7 Construction\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT` | `[arg_addrs…], argc, type` | `Variant::construct(type, *dst, argptrs, argc, err)` — unvalidated. |\n| `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_VALIDATED` | `[arg_addrs…], argc, ctor_idx` | `_constructors_ptr[ctor_idx](dst, argptrs)` — fast validated path. |\n| `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_ARRAY` | `[elem_addrs…], argc` | Builds an untyped `Array` from `argc` elements. |\n| `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_TYPED_ARRAY` | `[elem_addrs…], argc, script_type_addr, builtin_type, native_type_idx` | Builds a typed `Array`. |\n| `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_DICTIONARY` | `[k0_addr, v0_addr, …], argc` | Builds a `Dictionary`; operands alternate key/value; `argc` = number of pairs. |\n\nFor variable-argument instructions the VM first calls `LOAD_INSTRUCTION_ARGS`, which reads `_code_ptr[ip+1]` as the count, populates `instruction_args[]`, then advances `ip` past the address block.\n\n### 4.8 Function Calls\n\nAll call instructions use the `LOAD_INSTRUCTION_ARGS` / `GET_INSTRUCTION_ARG` protocol. In `instruction_args[]`:\n- Indices `0..argc-1` — function arguments\n- Index `argc` — base object (receiver)\n- Index `argc+1` — return value slot (when present)\n\n| Opcode | Post-args words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_CALL` | `argc, name_idx` | `base->callp(name, argptrs, argc, ret, err)` — return value discarded. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_RETURN` | `argc, name_idx` | Same but captures return into `instruction_args[argc+1]`. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_ASYNC` | `argc, name_idx` | Like `CALL_RETURN` but suppresses \"async without await\" error. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_UTILITY` | `argc, name_idx` | `Variant::call_utility_function(name, dst, argptrs, argc, err)` — global utility (`print`, `len`, etc.). |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_UTILITY_VALIDATED` | `argc, utility_idx` | `_utilities_ptr[utility_idx](dst, argptrs, argc)` |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_GDSCRIPT_UTILITY` | `argc, gds_util_idx` | GDScript-specific utilities via `_gds_utilities_ptr[]`. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_BUILTIN_TYPE_VALIDATED` | `argc, method_idx` | `_builtin_methods_ptr[method_idx](base, argptrs, argc, ret)` — method on a Variant built-in type. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_SELF_BASE` | `argc, name_idx` | Walks `_script->base` chain to invoke a parent-class GDScript method. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_METHOD_BIND` | `argc, method_idx` | `_methods_ptr[method_idx]->call(base_obj, argptrs, argc, err)` — no return. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_METHOD_BIND_RET` | `argc, method_idx` | Same, captures return. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_METHOD_BIND_VALIDATED_RETURN` | `argc, method_idx` | `method->validated_call(base_obj, argptrs, ret)` — bypasses `CallError` struct. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_METHOD_BIND_VALIDATED_NO_RETURN` | `argc, method_idx` | Same without return. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_BUILTIN_STATIC` | `builtin_type, name_idx, argc` | `Variant::call_static(builtin_type, name, argptrs, argc, ret, err)` |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_NATIVE_STATIC` | `method_idx, argc` | `_methods_ptr[method_idx]->call(nullptr, argptrs, argc, err)` |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_NATIVE_STATIC_VALIDATED_RETURN` | `argc, method_idx` | `method->validated_call(nullptr, argptrs, ret)` |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_NATIVE_STATIC_VALIDATED_NO_RETURN` | `argc, method_idx` | Same, discards return. |\n\n**Validated vs. unvalidated calls:** When the compiler can prove argument types match the method's signature exactly (`_can_use_validate_call()`, `gdscript_compiler.cpp:234`), it emits a `*_VALIDATED_*` opcode that bypasses `Callable::CallError` checking for performance.\n\n### 4.9 Async / Coroutine\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_AWAIT` | `signal_or_state_addr` | Suspends execution. If operand is a `Signal` or `GDScriptFunctionState`, connects a one-shot callback and returns a `GDScriptFunctionState` to the caller. If operand is an immediate value, skips `OPCODE_AWAIT_RESUME` and continues synchronously. |\n| `OPCODE_AWAIT_RESUME` | `result_addr` | Placed immediately after `OPCODE_AWAIT`. On resume, copies `p_state->result` into `*result`. |\n\n### 4.10 Lambda Creation\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_CREATE_LAMBDA` | `[capture_addrs…], captures_count, lambda_idx` | Creates `GDScriptLambdaCallable` closing over `captures_count` values. Result is a `Callable`. |\n| `OPCODE_CREATE_SELF_LAMBDA` | `[capture_addrs…], captures_count, lambda_idx` | Same but binds `self` via `GDScriptLambdaSelfCallable`. |\n\n### 4.11 Control Flow\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_JUMP` | `target` | `ip = target` (absolute code offset). |\n| `OPCODE_JUMP_IF` | `test_addr, target` | `if (test->booleanize()) ip = target` |\n| `OPCODE_JUMP_IF_NOT` | `test_addr, target` | `if (!test->booleanize()) ip = target` |\n| `OPCODE_JUMP_TO_DEF_ARGUMENT` | _(none)_ | `ip = _default_arg_ptr[defarg]` — jumps to the next missing default argument initializer. |\n| `OPCODE_JUMP_IF_SHARED` | `val_addr, target` | `if (val->is_shared()) ip = target` — copy-on-write check before mutation. |\n\n### 4.12 Return\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_RETURN` | `value_addr` | `retvalue = *r; OPCODE_BREAK` — exits the dispatch loop. |\n| `OPCODE_RETURN_TYPED_BUILTIN` | `value_addr, type` | Returns after type-checking / coercing to a built-in type. |\n| `OPCODE_RETURN_TYPED_ARRAY` | `value_addr, script_type_addr, builtin_type, native_type_idx` | Validates typed array before returning. |\n| `OPCODE_RETURN_TYPED_NATIVE` | `value_addr, native_class_addr` | Validates Object subclass. |\n| `OPCODE_RETURN_TYPED_SCRIPT` | `value_addr, script_addr` | Validates GDScript subtype. |\n\n### 4.13 Iteration (`for` loops)\n\n`for x in collection` compiles to `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_<TYPE>` (initialise iterator) followed by a loop body ending with `OPCODE_ITERATE_<TYPE>` (advance and check). Both share the format:\n\n```\nOPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_<TYPE>   counter_addr, container_addr, value_addr, exit_offset\nOPCODE_ITERATE_<TYPE>         counter_addr, container_addr, value_addr, exit_offset\n```\n\nWhen the iterator is exhausted the VM jumps `exit_offset` words forward (past the loop body). One pair of opcodes exists for each container type:\n\n| Type suffix | Container |\n|---|---|\n| _(none)_ | Generic `Variant` (dynamic dispatch) |\n| `_INT` | Integer range |\n| `_FLOAT` | Float range |\n| `_VECTOR2` / `_VECTOR2I` | `Vector2` / `Vector2i` |\n| `_VECTOR3` / `_VECTOR3I` | `Vector3` / `Vector3i` |\n| `_STRING` | `String` (character iteration) |\n| `_DICTIONARY` | `Dictionary` (key iteration) |\n| `_ARRAY` | `Array` |\n| `_PACKED_BYTE_ARRAY` | `PackedByteArray` |\n| `_PACKED_INT32_ARRAY` | `PackedInt32Array` |\n| `_PACKED_INT64_ARRAY` | `PackedInt64Array` |\n| `_PACKED_FLOAT32_ARRAY` | `PackedFloat32Array` |\n| `_PACKED_FLOAT64_ARRAY` | `PackedFloat64Array` |\n| `_PACKED_STRING_ARRAY` | `PackedStringArray` |\n| `_PACKED_VECTOR2_ARRAY` | `PackedVector2Array` |\n| `_PACKED_VECTOR3_ARRAY` | `PackedVector3Array` |\n| `_PACKED_COLOR_ARRAY` | `PackedColorArray` |\n| `_PACKED_VECTOR4_ARRAY` | `PackedVector4Array` |\n| `_OBJECT` | Objects implementing `_iter_init` / `_iter_next` / `_iter_get` |\n\n### 4.14 Global / Named Global Storage\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_STORE_GLOBAL` | `dst_addr, global_idx` | Copies a global constant (by integer index) into `*dst`. |\n| `OPCODE_STORE_NAMED_GLOBAL` | `dst_addr, name_idx` | Looks up a global by `StringName` in `GDScriptLanguage::get_singleton()->get_global_map()`. |\n\n### 4.15 Type Adjustment\n\nOne `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_<TYPE>` opcode exists for every `Variant::Type` value. It re-initialises a stack slot in-place so the slot holds the correct concrete C++ union member, needed when a temporary is reused across differently-typed expressions.\n\n```\nOPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_<TYPE>   target_addr\n```\n\nSemantics: `VariantInternal::initialize(target, Variant::TYPE_<TYPE>)`.\n\n### 4.16 Debug / Metadata\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_ASSERT` | `value_addr, message_addr` | Evaluates condition; prints message and breaks on failure. Compiled away in release builds. |\n| `OPCODE_BREAKPOINT` | _(none)_ | Triggers the debugger breakpoint handler. |\n| `OPCODE_LINE` | `line_number` | Records the current source line for the debugger and error messages. No runtime side-effects otherwise. |\n| `OPCODE_END` | _(none)_ | Marks the logical end of a function. Correct code never reaches this opcode at runtime. |\n\n---\n\n## 5. Function Call Convention\n\n### 5.1 Calling a GDScript Function\n\nEntry point: `GDScriptFunction::call()` (`gdscript_vm.cpp:448`).\n\n```cpp\nVariant call(GDScriptInstance *p_instance,\n             const Variant    **p_args,\n             int                p_argcount,\n             Callable::CallError &r_err,\n             CallState          *p_state = nullptr);\n```\n\n**Frame setup sequence (`gdscript_vm.cpp:511`):**\n\n1. Validate argument count; compute `defarg = _argument_count - p_argcount` for default-argument handling.\n2. `alloca_size = 3·sizeof(Variant*) + sizeof(Variant*)*_instruction_args_size + sizeof(Variant)*_stack_size`\n3. Arguments `p_args[0..p_argcount-1]` are placement-new'd into `stack[3..3+p_argcount-1]` with optional type coercion via `Variant::construct()`.\n4. Remaining slots `stack[p_argcount+3.._stack_size-1]` are default-initialised.\n5. `stack[0]` = `p_instance->owner` (self), `stack[1]` = `script`, `stack[2]` = `Variant()` (nil sentinel).\n6. Temporaries listed in `temporary_slots` are initialised via `type_init_function_table[type](&stack[slot])`.\n\n**Default arguments:**\n\nWhen `p_argcount < _argument_count`, `defarg > 0`. The VM starts executing normally but hits `OPCODE_JUMP_TO_DEF_ARGUMENT`, which sets `ip = _default_arg_ptr[defarg]`, jumping to the initialisation code for the next missing argument.\n\n**Return:**\n\n`OPCODE_RETURN` (or a typed variant) sets the stack-local `Variant retvalue` and breaks out of the dispatch loop. The return value is forwarded to the caller.\n\n**Recursion limit:**\n\nA thread-local `call_depth` counter is incremented on entry and decremented on exit. If it exceeds `MAX_CALL_DEPTH` (2 048), the call returns a default-constructed value and `r_err` is set.\n\n### 5.2 Calling a Native Method (MethodBind)\n\n- **`OPCODE_CALL_METHOD_BIND_RET`** — `method->call(base_obj, argptrs, argc, err)` with `Callable::CallError`.\n- **`OPCODE_CALL_METHOD_BIND_VALIDATED_RETURN`** — `method->validated_call(base_obj, argptrs, ret)` — faster, no error struct.\n\nThe compiler chooses the validated form when all argument types match the method signature exactly (`_can_use_validate_call()`, `gdscript_compiler.cpp:234`).\n\n### 5.3 Variable-Argument Instruction Protocol\n\nInstructions that accept a variable number of operands use a two-level scheme:\n\n1. **Load phase** (`LOAD_INSTRUCTION_ARGS` macro): reads `_code_ptr[ip+1]` as the argument count, calls `GET_VARIANT_PTR` for each address, populates `instruction_args[]`, then advances `ip` by that count.\n2. **Access phase** (`GET_INSTRUCTION_ARG(v, idx)`): `Variant *v = instruction_args[idx]`.\n\nAfter loading, `_code_ptr[ip + N]` refers to the fixed (non-address) parameters such as `argc`, method index, or type.\n\n---\n\n## 6. Local Variable and Member Variable Access\n\n### 6.1 Local Variables and Parameters\n\nFunction parameters and local variables reside in the flat stack array starting at index 3. Parameters occupy `stack[3], stack[4], …` in declaration order; locals take higher indices as assigned by `CodeGen`.\n\nThe compiler tracks them in `codegen.parameters` and `codegen.locals` (`gdscript_compiler.cpp:70`). When referenced, they resolve to `Address(ADDR_TYPE_STACK, idx)`.\n\n### 6.2 Instance Member Variables (GDScript fields)\n\nGDScript-level instance fields are stored in `GDScriptInstance::members[]` (`Vector<Variant>`). They are addressed directly via `ADDR_TYPE_MEMBER`:\n\n```\nencoded_address = member_index | (ADDR_TYPE_MEMBER << ADDR_BITS)\n```\n\nAt runtime, `variant_addresses[ADDR_TYPE_MEMBER] = p_instance->members.ptrw()`.\n\n### 6.3 Native (C++) Properties\n\nNative properties registered with `ClassDB` are accessed via `OPCODE_GET_MEMBER` / `OPCODE_SET_MEMBER`, which call `ClassDB::get_property()` / `ClassDB::set_property()` on `p_instance->owner`.\n\nWhen a GDScript member has a custom getter/setter, the compiler emits a self-call (`write_call_self`) to invoke the accessor rather than accessing the backing slot directly (`gdscript_compiler.cpp:303`).\n\n### 6.4 Static Variables\n\nGDScript static variables live in `GDScript::static_variables[]`. They are accessed via `OPCODE_GET_STATIC_VARIABLE` / `OPCODE_SET_STATIC_VARIABLE`, which locate the owning `GDScript` object from `stack[ADDR_STACK_CLASS]` and index into its array.\n\n### 6.5 Constants\n\nCompile-time constants (literals, folded expressions) are stored in `GDScriptFunction::constants[]` and referenced via `ADDR_TYPE_CONSTANT` addresses. They are read-only during execution.\n\n---\n\n## 7. Dispatch Loop Implementation\n\nOn GCC/Clang the VM uses a **computed-goto dispatch table** (`OPCODES_TABLE` macro, `gdscript_vm.cpp:214`):\n\n```c\nstatic const void *switch_table_ops[] = { &&OPCODE_OPERATOR, &&OPCODE_OPERATOR_VALIDATED, … };\n// At each opcode end:\ngoto *switch_table_ops[_code_ptr[ip]];\n```\n\nOn MSVC (and as fallback) a `switch` statement is used. Both paths are abstracted by the `OPCODE`, `OPCODE_SWITCH`, `DISPATCH_OPCODE`, and related macros.\n\nOuter loop guard:\n- **Debug builds:** `while (ip < _code_size)` — bounds-checked.\n- **Release builds:** `while (true)` — relies on `OPCODE_RETURN` / `OPCODE_END` to exit.\n\n---\n\n## 8. Coroutine / Await Suspension\n\nWhen `OPCODE_AWAIT` suspends a function, the entire execution state is captured into a heap-allocated `GDScriptFunctionState` (`gdscript_function.h:558`):\n\n```cpp\nstruct CallState {\n    GDScript         *script;\n    GDScriptInstance *instance;\n    Vector<uint8_t>   stack;   // serialised Variant array\n    int               stack_size, ip, line, defarg;\n    Variant           result;  // value injected on resume\n};\n```\n\nStack slots 3 through `_stack_size-1` are placement-new'd into `gdfs->state.stack` (`gdscript_vm.cpp:2397`). On `GDScriptFunctionState::resume()`, the state is passed back as `p_state` and the VM restores the frame, continuing at `ip` pointing to `OPCODE_AWAIT_RESUME`.\n\n---\n\n## 9. Opcode Category Summary\n\n| Category | Opcodes |\n|---|---|\n| Arithmetic / bitwise / comparison | `OPCODE_OPERATOR`, `OPCODE_OPERATOR_VALIDATED` |\n| Type tests (`is`) | `OPCODE_TYPE_TEST_BUILTIN/ARRAY/NATIVE/SCRIPT` |\n| Key/index get | `OPCODE_GET_KEYED`, `OPCODE_GET_KEYED_VALIDATED`, `OPCODE_GET_INDEXED_VALIDATED` |\n| Key/index set | `OPCODE_SET_KEYED`, `OPCODE_SET_KEYED_VALIDATED`, `OPCODE_SET_INDEXED_VALIDATED` |\n| Named property get | `OPCODE_GET_NAMED`, `OPCODE_GET_NAMED_VALIDATED` |\n| Named property set | `OPCODE_SET_NAMED`, `OPCODE_SET_NAMED_VALIDATED` |\n| Member / static variable | `OPCODE_{GET,SET}_MEMBER`, `OPCODE_{GET,SET}_STATIC_VARIABLE` |\n| Assignment | `OPCODE_ASSIGN*` — 8 variants |\n| Type cast | `OPCODE_CAST_TO_BUILTIN/NATIVE/SCRIPT` |\n| Construction | `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT`, `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_VALIDATED`, `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_ARRAY`, `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_TYPED_ARRAY`, `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_DICTIONARY` |\n| Method calls | `OPCODE_CALL*` — 16 variants |\n| Async / coroutine | `OPCODE_AWAIT`, `OPCODE_AWAIT_RESUME` |\n| Lambda creation | `OPCODE_CREATE_LAMBDA`, `OPCODE_CREATE_SELF_LAMBDA` |\n| Control flow | `OPCODE_JUMP*` — 5 variants |\n| Return | `OPCODE_RETURN*` — 5 variants |\n| Iteration | `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_*` / `OPCODE_ITERATE_*` — 21 type-specific pairs |\n| Global storage | `OPCODE_STORE_GLOBAL`, `OPCODE_STORE_NAMED_GLOBAL` |\n| Type adjustment | `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_*` — 29 variants (one per `Variant::Type`) |\n| Debug / metadata | `OPCODE_ASSERT`, `OPCODE_BREAKPOINT`, `OPCODE_LINE`, `OPCODE_END` VM Architecture\n\nThe GDScript virtual machine is **register-based with a flat Variant array** (called \"the stack\" in source, but operands are addressed by index rather than pushed/popped).\n\nKey characteristics:\n\n| Property | Value |\n|---|---|\n| Architecture | Register / flat-array (not a push-pop stack) |\n| Value type | `Variant` (tagged union covering all GDScript types) |\n| Word size | `int` (32-bit opcode words) |\n| Instruction pointer | Integer index `ip` into `_code_ptr[]` |\n| Max call depth | 2 048 frames (enforced per-thread) |\n| Dispatch | Computed-goto table on GCC; `switch` on MSVC |\n\n### Runtime Layout\n\nAt function entry the VM allocates a single contiguous block via `alloca()`:\n\n```\n[0 .. _stack_size-1]                 Variant[_stack_size]              (working registers)\n[sizeof(Variant)*_stack_size ...]    Variant*[_instruction_args_size]  (per-instruction arg pointer array)\n```\n\nThe first three stack slots are **fixed** (see §3); user registers begin at slot 3.\n\n---\n\n## 2. Address Encoding\n\nEvery operand word in the bytecode stream encodes both the storage class and the index:\n\n```\n  bits 31..24      bits 23..0\n ┌────────────┬────────────────────────────┐\n │ addr_type  │      addr_index (24 bits)  │\n └────────────┴────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\nConstants from `GDScriptFunction::Address` (`gdscript_function.h:373`):\n\n| Constant | Value | Meaning |\n|---|---|---|\n| `ADDR_BITS` | 24 | Index occupies the low 24 bits |\n| `ADDR_MASK` | `(1<<24)-1` | Mask for the index |\n| `ADDR_TYPE_MASK` | `~ADDR_MASK` | Mask for the type tag |\n| `ADDR_TYPE_STACK` | 0 | Operand lives in the stack/register array |\n| `ADDR_TYPE_CONSTANT` | 1 | Operand is a compile-time constant (`_constants_ptr[]`) |\n| `ADDR_TYPE_MEMBER` | 2 | Operand is an instance member (`p_instance->members[]`) |\n| `ADDR_TYPE_MAX` | 3 | Sentinel |\n\nAt runtime the macro `GET_VARIANT_PTR(name, offset)` decodes `_code_ptr[ip + 1 + offset]` into a `Variant*` by indexing the appropriate array.\n\n### Fixed Stack Addresses\n\n```\nADDR_STACK_SELF  = 0   →  stack[0] = p_instance->owner  (Object*)\nADDR_STACK_CLASS = 1   →  stack[1] = script              (GDScript*)\nADDR_STACK_NIL   = 2   →  stack[2] = Variant()           (null sentinel)\n```\n\nUser locals and temporaries start at stack index 3.\n\n---\n\n## 3. Variant Type System\n\nAll values are `Variant` instances. The `Variant::Type` enum (from `core/variant/variant.h`) includes:\n\n| Type ID | Name | Notes |\n|---|---|---|\n| 0 | `NIL` | null / unset |\n| 1 | `BOOL` | |\n| 2 | `INT` | `int64_t` |\n| 3 | `FLOAT` | `double` |\n| 4 | `STRING` | |\n| 5–13 | `VECTOR2` … `VECTOR4I` | Math types |\n| 14–19 | `PLANE` … `PROJECTION` | 3-D geometry |\n| 20 | `COLOR` | |\n| 21 | `STRING_NAME` | |\n| 22 | `NODE_PATH` | |\n| 23 | `RID` | |\n| 24 | `OBJECT` | `Object*` (ref-counted or not) |\n| 25 | `CALLABLE` | |\n| 26 | `SIGNAL` | |\n| 27 | `DICTIONARY` | |\n| 28 | `ARRAY` | Optionally typed |\n| 29–38 | `PACKED_*_ARRAY` | Typed contiguous arrays |\n\nType-checking is performed by `GDScriptDataType::is_type()` (`gdscript_function.h:67`). The descriptor's `kind` field distinguishes `BUILTIN`, `NATIVE`, `SCRIPT`, and `GDSCRIPT`.\n\n---\n\n## 4. Complete Opcode Table\n\nOpcodes are defined as `GDScriptFunction::Opcode` (`gdscript_function.h:218`). Each entry shows:\n- **Operand words** after the opcode word (addresses use `GET_VARIANT_PTR`; plain `int` values appear literally in `_code_ptr[]`)\n- **Semantics** derived from the dispatch loop in `gdscript_vm.cpp`\n\n### 4.1 Arithmetic / Bitwise / Comparison Operators\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_OPERATOR` | `a_addr, b_addr, dst_addr, op, sig_cache, ret_type_cache, func_ptr…` | `*dst = *a OP *b`. `op` is `Variant::Operator`. Inline-caches the validated evaluator on first execution; falls back to `Variant::evaluate()` on type mismatch. |\n| `OPCODE_OPERATOR_VALIDATED` | `a_addr, b_addr, dst_addr, func_idx` | Pre-validated fast path: `_operator_funcs_ptr[func_idx](a, b, dst)`. |\n\n`Variant::Operator` values include: `OP_ADD`, `OP_SUBTRACT`, `OP_MULTIPLY`, `OP_DIVIDE`, `OP_MODULE`, `OP_EQUAL`, `OP_NOT_EQUAL`, `OP_LESS`, `OP_LESS_EQUAL`, `OP_GREATER`, `OP_GREATER_EQUAL`, `OP_AND`, `OP_OR`, `OP_NOT`, `OP_IN`, `OP_SHIFT_LEFT`, `OP_SHIFT_RIGHT`, `OP_BIT_AND`, `OP_BIT_OR`, `OP_BIT_XOR`, `OP_BIT_NEGATE`.\n\n### 4.2 Type Tests (`is` operator)\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_TYPE_TEST_BUILTIN` | `dst_addr, value_addr, builtin_type` | `*dst = (value->get_type() == builtin_type)` |\n| `OPCODE_TYPE_TEST_ARRAY` | `dst_addr, value_addr, script_type_addr, builtin_type, native_type_idx` | Tests typed-array element type (builtin type + native class + script). |\n| `OPCODE_TYPE_TEST_NATIVE` | `dst_addr, value_addr, native_type_idx` | `*dst = ClassDB::is_parent_class(obj->class_name, native_type)` |\n| `OPCODE_TYPE_TEST_SCRIPT` | `dst_addr, value_addr, type_addr` | Walks the script inheritance chain. |\n\n### 4.3 Key / Index / Named Access\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_GET_KEYED` | `src_addr, index_addr, dst_addr` | `*dst = src->get(*index)` — dynamic/slow path. |\n| `OPCODE_GET_KEYED_VALIDATED` | `src_addr, key_addr, dst_addr, getter_idx` | `_keyed_getters_ptr[getter_idx](src, key, dst, &valid)` |\n| `OPCODE_GET_INDEXED_VALIDATED` | `src_addr, index_addr, dst_addr, getter_idx` | Integer-indexed fast path. |\n| `OPCODE_SET_KEYED` | `dst_addr, index_addr, value_addr` | `dst->set(*index, *value)` |\n| `OPCODE_SET_KEYED_VALIDATED` | `dst_addr, index_addr, value_addr, setter_idx` | `_keyed_setters_ptr[setter_idx](dst, index, value, &valid)` |\n| `OPCODE_SET_INDEXED_VALIDATED` | `dst_addr, index_addr, value_addr, setter_idx` | Integer-indexed; checks out-of-bounds. |\n| `OPCODE_GET_NAMED` | `src_addr, dst_addr, name_idx` | `*dst = src->get_named(_global_names_ptr[name_idx])` |\n| `OPCODE_GET_NAMED_VALIDATED` | `src_addr, dst_addr, getter_idx` | `_getters_ptr[getter_idx](src, dst)` |\n| `OPCODE_SET_NAMED` | `dst_addr, value_addr, name_idx` | `dst->set_named(_global_names_ptr[name_idx], *value)` |\n| `OPCODE_SET_NAMED_VALIDATED` | `dst_addr, value_addr, setter_idx` | `_setters_ptr[setter_idx](dst, value)` |\n\n`_global_names_ptr[]` is a compile-time `StringName[]` table embedded in the function object.\n\n### 4.4 Member / Static Variable Access\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_GET_MEMBER` | `dst_addr, name_idx` | `ClassDB::get_property(p_instance->owner, name, *dst)` — native C++ property getter. |\n| `OPCODE_SET_MEMBER` | `src_addr, name_idx` | `ClassDB::set_property(p_instance->owner, name, *src)` |\n| `OPCODE_GET_STATIC_VARIABLE` | `target_addr, class_addr, var_idx` | `*target = gdscript->static_variables[var_idx]` |\n| `OPCODE_SET_STATIC_VARIABLE` | `value_addr, class_addr, var_idx` | `gdscript->static_variables[var_idx] = *value` |\n\nGDScript-level instance fields are accessed via `ADDR_TYPE_MEMBER` addressing directly (not through these opcodes). `GET_MEMBER`/`SET_MEMBER` are for **native (C++) properties** registered with `ClassDB`.\n\n### 4.5 Assignment\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN` | `dst_addr, src_addr` | `*dst = *src` |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_NULL` | `dst_addr` | `*dst = Variant()` |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_TRUE` | `dst_addr` | `*dst = true` |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_FALSE` | `dst_addr` | `*dst = false` |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_TYPED_BUILTIN` | `dst_addr, src_addr, type` | Type-checked copy; constructs via `Variant::construct()` if types differ. |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_TYPED_ARRAY` | `dst_addr, src_addr, script_type_addr, builtin_type, native_type_idx` | Verifies typed-array element type before copying. |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_TYPED_NATIVE` | `dst_addr, src_addr, native_class_addr` | Verifies object is an instance of the native class. |\n| `OPCODE_ASSIGN_TYPED_SCRIPT` | `dst_addr, src_addr, script_addr` | Walks GDScript inheritance chain to verify compatibility. |\n\n### 4.6 Type Casts\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_CAST_TO_BUILTIN` | `src_addr, dst_addr, type` | `Variant::construct(type, *dst, &src, 1, err)` |\n| `OPCODE_CAST_TO_NATIVE` | `src_addr, dst_addr, native_class_addr` | Sets `*dst = null` if object doesn't inherit the target class; otherwise copies. |\n| `OPCODE_CAST_TO_SCRIPT` | `src_addr, dst_addr, script_addr` | Same semantics for GDScript types. |\n\n### 4.7 Construction\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT` | `[arg_addrs…], argc, type` | `Variant::construct(type, *dst, argptrs, argc, err)` — unvalidated. |\n| `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_VALIDATED` | `[arg_addrs…], argc, ctor_idx` | `_constructors_ptr[ctor_idx](dst, argptrs)` — fast validated path. |\n| `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_ARRAY` | `[elem_addrs…], argc` | Builds an untyped `Array` from `argc` elements. |\n| `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_TYPED_ARRAY` | `[elem_addrs…], argc, script_type_addr, builtin_type, native_type_idx` | Builds a typed `Array`. |\n| `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_DICTIONARY` | `[k0_addr, v0_addr, …], argc` | Builds a `Dictionary`; operands alternate key/value; `argc` = number of pairs. |\n\nFor variable-argument instructions the VM first calls `LOAD_INSTRUCTION_ARGS`, which reads `_code_ptr[ip+1]` as the count, populates `instruction_args[]`, then advances `ip` past the address block.\n\n### 4.8 Function Calls\n\nAll call instructions use the `LOAD_INSTRUCTION_ARGS` / `GET_INSTRUCTION_ARG` protocol. In `instruction_args[]`:\n- Indices `0..argc-1` — function arguments\n- Index `argc` — base object (receiver)\n- Index `argc+1` — return value slot (when present)\n\n| Opcode | Post-args words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_CALL` | `argc, name_idx` | `base->callp(name, argptrs, argc, ret, err)` — return value discarded. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_RETURN` | `argc, name_idx` | Same but captures return into `instruction_args[argc+1]`. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_ASYNC` | `argc, name_idx` | Like `CALL_RETURN` but suppresses \"async without await\" error. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_UTILITY` | `argc, name_idx` | `Variant::call_utility_function(name, dst, argptrs, argc, err)` — global utility (`print`, `len`, etc.). |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_UTILITY_VALIDATED` | `argc, utility_idx` | `_utilities_ptr[utility_idx](dst, argptrs, argc)` |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_GDSCRIPT_UTILITY` | `argc, gds_util_idx` | GDScript-specific utilities via `_gds_utilities_ptr[]`. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_BUILTIN_TYPE_VALIDATED` | `argc, method_idx` | `_builtin_methods_ptr[method_idx](base, argptrs, argc, ret)` — method on a Variant built-in type. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_SELF_BASE` | `argc, name_idx` | Walks `_script->base` chain to invoke a parent-class GDScript method. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_METHOD_BIND` | `argc, method_idx` | `_methods_ptr[method_idx]->call(base_obj, argptrs, argc, err)` — no return. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_METHOD_BIND_RET` | `argc, method_idx` | Same, captures return. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_METHOD_BIND_VALIDATED_RETURN` | `argc, method_idx` | `method->validated_call(base_obj, argptrs, ret)` — bypasses `CallError` struct. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_METHOD_BIND_VALIDATED_NO_RETURN` | `argc, method_idx` | Same without return. |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_BUILTIN_STATIC` | `builtin_type, name_idx, argc` | `Variant::call_static(builtin_type, name, argptrs, argc, ret, err)` |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_NATIVE_STATIC` | `method_idx, argc` | `_methods_ptr[method_idx]->call(nullptr, argptrs, argc, err)` |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_NATIVE_STATIC_VALIDATED_RETURN` | `argc, method_idx` | `method->validated_call(nullptr, argptrs, ret)` |\n| `OPCODE_CALL_NATIVE_STATIC_VALIDATED_NO_RETURN` | `argc, method_idx` | Same, discards return. |\n\n**Validated vs. unvalidated calls:** When the compiler can prove argument types match the method's signature exactly (`_can_use_validate_call()`, `gdscript_compiler.cpp:234`), it emits a `*_VALIDATED_*` opcode that bypasses `Callable::CallError` checking for performance.\n\n### 4.9 Async / Coroutine\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_AWAIT` | `signal_or_state_addr` | Suspends execution. If operand is a `Signal` or `GDScriptFunctionState`, connects a one-shot callback and returns a `GDScriptFunctionState` to the caller. If operand is an immediate value, skips `OPCODE_AWAIT_RESUME` and continues synchronously. |\n| `OPCODE_AWAIT_RESUME` | `result_addr` | Placed immediately after `OPCODE_AWAIT`. On resume, copies `p_state->result` into `*result`. |\n\n### 4.10 Lambda Creation\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_CREATE_LAMBDA` | `[capture_addrs…], captures_count, lambda_idx` | Creates `GDScriptLambdaCallable` closing over `captures_count` values. Result is a `Callable`. |\n| `OPCODE_CREATE_SELF_LAMBDA` | `[capture_addrs…], captures_count, lambda_idx` | Same but binds `self` via `GDScriptLambdaSelfCallable`. |\n\n### 4.11 Control Flow\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_JUMP` | `target` | `ip = target` (absolute code offset). |\n| `OPCODE_JUMP_IF` | `test_addr, target` | `if (test->booleanize()) ip = target` |\n| `OPCODE_JUMP_IF_NOT` | `test_addr, target` | `if (!test->booleanize()) ip = target` |\n| `OPCODE_JUMP_TO_DEF_ARGUMENT` | _(none)_ | `ip = _default_arg_ptr[defarg]` — jumps to the next missing default argument initializer. |\n| `OPCODE_JUMP_IF_SHARED` | `val_addr, target` | `if (val->is_shared()) ip = target` — copy-on-write check before mutation. |\n\n### 4.12 Return\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_RETURN` | `value_addr` | `retvalue = *r; OPCODE_BREAK` — exits the dispatch loop. |\n| `OPCODE_RETURN_TYPED_BUILTIN` | `value_addr, type` | Returns after type-checking / coercing to a built-in type. |\n| `OPCODE_RETURN_TYPED_ARRAY` | `value_addr, script_type_addr, builtin_type, native_type_idx` | Validates typed array before returning. |\n| `OPCODE_RETURN_TYPED_NATIVE` | `value_addr, native_class_addr` | Validates Object subclass. |\n| `OPCODE_RETURN_TYPED_SCRIPT` | `value_addr, script_addr` | Validates GDScript subtype. |\n\n### 4.13 Iteration (`for` loops)\n\n`for x in collection` compiles to `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_<TYPE>` (initialise iterator) followed by a loop body ending with `OPCODE_ITERATE_<TYPE>` (advance and check). Both share the format:\n\n```\nOPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_<TYPE>   counter_addr, container_addr, value_addr, exit_offset\nOPCODE_ITERATE_<TYPE>         counter_addr, container_addr, value_addr, exit_offset\n```\n\nWhen the iterator is exhausted the VM jumps `exit_offset` words forward (past the loop body). One pair of opcodes exists for each container type:\n\n| Type suffix | Container |\n|---|---|\n| _(none)_ | Generic `Variant` (dynamic dispatch) |\n| `_INT` | Integer range |\n| `_FLOAT` | Float range |\n| `_VECTOR2` / `_VECTOR2I` | `Vector2` / `Vector2i` |\n| `_VECTOR3` / `_VECTOR3I` | `Vector3` / `Vector3i` |\n| `_STRING` | `String` (character iteration) |\n| `_DICTIONARY` | `Dictionary` (key iteration) |\n| `_ARRAY` | `Array` |\n| `_PACKED_BYTE_ARRAY` | `PackedByteArray` |\n| `_PACKED_INT32_ARRAY` | `PackedInt32Array` |\n| `_PACKED_INT64_ARRAY` | `PackedInt64Array` |\n| `_PACKED_FLOAT32_ARRAY` | `PackedFloat32Array` |\n| `_PACKED_FLOAT64_ARRAY` | `PackedFloat64Array` |\n| `_PACKED_STRING_ARRAY` | `PackedStringArray` |\n| `_PACKED_VECTOR2_ARRAY` | `PackedVector2Array` |\n| `_PACKED_VECTOR3_ARRAY` | `PackedVector3Array` |\n| `_PACKED_COLOR_ARRAY` | `PackedColorArray` |\n| `_PACKED_VECTOR4_ARRAY` | `PackedVector4Array` |\n| `_OBJECT` | Objects implementing `_iter_init` / `_iter_next` / `_iter_get` |\n\n### 4.14 Global / Named Global Storage\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_STORE_GLOBAL` | `dst_addr, global_idx` | Copies a global constant (by integer index) into `*dst`. |\n| `OPCODE_STORE_NAMED_GLOBAL` | `dst_addr, name_idx` | Looks up a global by `StringName` in `GDScriptLanguage::get_singleton()->get_global_map()`. |\n\n### 4.15 Type Adjustment\n\nOne `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_<TYPE>` opcode exists for every `Variant::Type` value. It re-initialises a stack slot in-place so the slot holds the correct concrete C++ union member, needed when a temporary is reused across differently-typed expressions.\n\n```\nOPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_<TYPE>   target_addr\n```\n\nSemantics: `VariantInternal::initialize(target, Variant::TYPE_<TYPE>)`.\n\n### 4.16 Debug / Metadata\n\n| Opcode | Operand words | Semantics |\n|---|---|---|\n| `OPCODE_ASSERT` | `value_addr, message_addr` | Evaluates condition; prints message and breaks on failure. Compiled away in release builds. |\n| `OPCODE_BREAKPOINT` | _(none)_ | Triggers the debugger breakpoint handler. |\n| `OPCODE_LINE` | `line_number` | Records the current source line for the debugger and error messages. No runtime side-effects otherwise. |\n| `OPCODE_END` | _(none)_ | Marks the logical end of a function. Correct code never reaches this opcode at runtime. |\n\n---\n\n## 5. Function Call Convention\n\n### 5.1 Calling a GDScript Function\n\nEntry point: `GDScriptFunction::call()` (`gdscript_vm.cpp:448`).\n\n```cpp\nVariant call(GDScriptInstance *p_instance,\n             const Variant    **p_args,\n             int                p_argcount,\n             Callable::CallError &r_err,\n             CallState          *p_state = nullptr);\n```\n\n**Frame setup sequence (`gdscript_vm.cpp:511`):**\n\n1. Validate argument count; compute `defarg = _argument_count - p_argcount` for default-argument handling.\n2. `alloca_size = 3·sizeof(Variant*) + sizeof(Variant*)*_instruction_args_size + sizeof(Variant)*_stack_size`\n3. Arguments `p_args[0..p_argcount-1]` are placement-new'd into `stack[3..3+p_argcount-1]` with optional type coercion via `Variant::construct()`.\n4. Remaining slots `stack[p_argcount+3.._stack_size-1]` are default-initialised.\n5. `stack[0]` = `p_instance->owner` (self), `stack[1]` = `script`, `stack[2]` = `Variant()` (nil sentinel).\n6. Temporaries listed in `temporary_slots` are initialised via `type_init_function_table[type](&stack[slot])`.\n\n**Default arguments:**\n\nWhen `p_argcount < _argument_count`, `defarg > 0`. The VM starts executing normally but hits `OPCODE_JUMP_TO_DEF_ARGUMENT`, which sets `ip = _default_arg_ptr[defarg]`, jumping to the initialisation code for the next missing argument.\n\n**Return:**\n\n`OPCODE_RETURN` (or a typed variant) sets the stack-local `Variant retvalue` and breaks out of the dispatch loop. The return value is forwarded to the caller.\n\n**Recursion limit:**\n\nA thread-local `call_depth` counter is incremented on entry and decremented on exit. If it exceeds `MAX_CALL_DEPTH` (2 048), the call returns a default-constructed value and `r_err` is set.\n\n### 5.2 Calling a Native Method (MethodBind)\n\n- **`OPCODE_CALL_METHOD_BIND_RET`** — `method->call(base_obj, argptrs, argc, err)` with `Callable::CallError`.\n- **`OPCODE_CALL_METHOD_BIND_VALIDATED_RETURN`** — `method->validated_call(base_obj, argptrs, ret)` — faster, no error struct.\n\nThe compiler chooses the validated form when all argument types match the method signature exactly (`_can_use_validate_call()`, `gdscript_compiler.cpp:234`).\n\n### 5.3 Variable-Argument Instruction Protocol\n\nInstructions that accept a variable number of operands use a two-level scheme:\n\n1. **Load phase** (`LOAD_INSTRUCTION_ARGS` macro): reads `_code_ptr[ip+1]` as the argument count, calls `GET_VARIANT_PTR` for each address, populates `instruction_args[]`, then advances `ip` by that count.\n2. **Access phase** (`GET_INSTRUCTION_ARG(v, idx)`): `Variant *v = instruction_args[idx]`.\n\nAfter loading, `_code_ptr[ip + N]` refers to the fixed (non-address) parameters such as `argc`, method index, or type.\n\n---\n\n## 6. Local Variable and Member Variable Access\n\n### 6.1 Local Variables and Parameters\n\nFunction parameters and local variables reside in the flat stack array starting at index 3. Parameters occupy `stack[3], stack[4], …` in declaration order; locals take higher indices as assigned by `CodeGen`.\n\nThe compiler tracks them in `codegen.parameters` and `codegen.locals` (`gdscript_compiler.cpp:70`). When referenced, they resolve to `Address(ADDR_TYPE_STACK, idx)`.\n\n### 6.2 Instance Member Variables (GDScript fields)\n\nGDScript-level instance fields are stored in `GDScriptInstance::members[]` (`Vector<Variant>`). They are addressed directly via `ADDR_TYPE_MEMBER`:\n\n```\nencoded_address = member_index | (ADDR_TYPE_MEMBER << ADDR_BITS)\n```\n\nAt runtime, `variant_addresses[ADDR_TYPE_MEMBER] = p_instance->members.ptrw()`.\n\n### 6.3 Native (C++) Properties\n\nNative properties registered with `ClassDB` are accessed via `OPCODE_GET_MEMBER` / `OPCODE_SET_MEMBER`, which call `ClassDB::get_property()` / `ClassDB::set_property()` on `p_instance->owner`.\n\nWhen a GDScript member has a custom getter/setter, the compiler emits a self-call (`write_call_self`) to invoke the accessor rather than accessing the backing slot directly (`gdscript_compiler.cpp:303`).\n\n### 6.4 Static Variables\n\nGDScript static variables live in `GDScript::static_variables[]`. They are accessed via `OPCODE_GET_STATIC_VARIABLE` / `OPCODE_SET_STATIC_VARIABLE`, which locate the owning `GDScript` object from `stack[ADDR_STACK_CLASS]` and index into its array.\n\n### 6.5 Constants\n\nCompile-time constants (literals, folded expressions) are stored in `GDScriptFunction::constants[]` and referenced via `ADDR_TYPE_CONSTANT` addresses. They are read-only during execution.\n\n---\n\n## 7. Dispatch Loop Implementation\n\nOn GCC/Clang the VM uses a **computed-goto dispatch table** (`OPCODES_TABLE` macro, `gdscript_vm.cpp:214`):\n\n```c\nstatic const void *switch_table_ops[] = { &&OPCODE_OPERATOR, &&OPCODE_OPERATOR_VALIDATED, … };\n// At each opcode end:\ngoto *switch_table_ops[_code_ptr[ip]];\n```\n\nOn MSVC (and as fallback) a `switch` statement is used. Both paths are abstracted by the `OPCODE`, `OPCODE_SWITCH`, `DISPATCH_OPCODE`, and related macros.\n\nOuter loop guard:\n- **Debug builds:** `while (ip < _code_size)` — bounds-checked.\n- **Release builds:** `while (true)` — relies on `OPCODE_RETURN` / `OPCODE_END` to exit.\n\n---\n\n## 8. Coroutine / Await Suspension\n\nWhen `OPCODE_AWAIT` suspends a function, the entire execution state is captured into a heap-allocated `GDScriptFunctionState` (`gdscript_function.h:558`):\n\n```cpp\nstruct CallState {\n    GDScript         *script;\n    GDScriptInstance *instance;\n    Vector<uint8_t>   stack;   // serialised Variant array\n    int               stack_size, ip, line, defarg;\n    Variant           result;  // value injected on resume\n};\n```\n\nStack slots 3 through `_stack_size-1` are placement-new'd into `gdfs->state.stack` (`gdscript_vm.cpp:2397`). On `GDScriptFunctionState::resume()`, the state is passed back as `p_state` and the VM restores the frame, continuing at `ip` pointing to `OPCODE_AWAIT_RESUME`.\n\n---\n\n## 9. Opcode Category Summary\n\n| Category | Opcodes |\n|---|---|\n| Arithmetic / bitwise / comparison | `OPCODE_OPERATOR`, `OPCODE_OPERATOR_VALIDATED` |\n| Type tests (`is`) | `OPCODE_TYPE_TEST_BUILTIN/ARRAY/NATIVE/SCRIPT` |\n| Key/index get | `OPCODE_GET_KEYED`, `OPCODE_GET_KEYED_VALIDATED`, `OPCODE_GET_INDEXED_VALIDATED` |\n| Key/index set | `OPCODE_SET_KEYED`, `OPCODE_SET_KEYED_VALIDATED`, `OPCODE_SET_INDEXED_VALIDATED` |\n| Named property get | `OPCODE_GET_NAMED`, `OPCODE_GET_NAMED_VALIDATED` |\n| Named property set | `OPCODE_SET_NAMED`, `OPCODE_SET_NAMED_VALIDATED` |\n| Member / static variable | `OPCODE_{GET,SET}_MEMBER`, `OPCODE_{GET,SET}_STATIC_VARIABLE` |\n| Assignment | `OPCODE_ASSIGN*` — 8 variants |\n| Type cast | `OPCODE_CAST_TO_BUILTIN/NATIVE/SCRIPT` |\n| Construction | `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT`, `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_VALIDATED`, `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_ARRAY`, `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_TYPED_ARRAY`, `OPCODE_CONSTRUCT_DICTIONARY` |\n| Method calls | `OPCODE_CALL*` — 16 variants |\n| Async / coroutine | `OPCODE_AWAIT`, `OPCODE_AWAIT_RESUME` |\n| Lambda creation | `OPCODE_CREATE_LAMBDA`, `OPCODE_CREATE_SELF_LAMBDA` |\n| Control flow | `OPCODE_JUMP*` — 5 variants |\n| Return | `OPCODE_RETURN*` — 5 variants |\n| Iteration | `OPCODE_ITERATE_BEGIN_*` / `OPCODE_ITERATE_*` — 21 type-specific pairs |\n| Global storage | `OPCODE_STORE_GLOBAL`, `OPCODE_STORE_NAMED_GLOBAL` |\n| Type adjustment | `OPCODE_TYPE_ADJUST_*` — 29 variants (one per `Variant::Type`) |\n| Debug / metadata | `OPCODE_ASSERT`, `OPCODE_BREAKPOINT`, `OPCODE_LINE`, `OPCODE_END` |\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
